Don't buy the Apple Watch Base Station.

That said, the quality of the product and the packaging in second-to-none.  The braided power cord is adds to the reassurance that this is a well-built product.  That said, I spend waaaay too much time searching for a coil.  With my watch, AirPods and phone, I truly needed every coil and I was embarrased, rather than proud of how easy it was to charge my devices.  It was like looking for a needle in a haystack--blindfolded.

After a couple weeks, I gave up and I've paid for return shipping from Canada and have already taken delivery of a SliceJuice Pro.  It doesn't feel as solid as Nomad's Base Station, but it's much easier to line things up with its six coils and it's cheaper.  I have yet to see whether I will be getting a refund on my return.

Sorry, Nomad--I really wanted it to work but it's not me; it's you.

Add a few more coils and I'll be glad to come back.<//Text>
